   1: """I-arch-001b — synthesize a v30.1 per_query_report_contract from a v6 template.
   2: 
   3: Input: v6 template JSON (config/v6_templates/<template_id>.json), query_slug.
   4: Output: {query_slug: <v30.1 contract dict>} ready to merge into a scope
   5: template's `per_query_report_contract` key, where M-55 frame_compiler and
   6: load_report_contract_for_slug both consume it.
   7: 
   8: Per Codex APPROVE iter 5: every entity carries a concrete http(s) url_pattern
   9: from T1 + a stable anchor; this satisfies M-56's `_fetch_url_pattern()` which
  10: treats the value as a literal URL, not a regex.
  11: """
  12: 
  13: from __future__ import annotations
  14: 
  15: import hashlib
  16: from typing import Any
  17: 
  18: # Per-template defaults for the type discriminator + identifier field names.
  19: # Codex iter-2: rolled clinical→drug/condition into a generic "frame" entity-
  20: # type so the v30 compiler doesn't try to dispatch on type-specific paths
  21: # that don't exist for synthesized contracts.
  22: _TYPE_FOR_TEMPLATE: dict[str, str] = {
  23:     "clinical": "drug",
  24:     "ai_sovereignty": "policy",
  25:     "canada_us": "policy",
  26:     "climate": "policy",
  27:     "defense": "policy",
  28:     "housing": "policy",
  29:     "trade": "policy",
  30:     "workforce": "policy",
  31: }
  32: 
  33: _REQUIRED_FIELDS_FOR_TEMPLATE: dict[str, list[str]] = {
  34:     "clinical": ["rxcui", "drugbank_id", "icd_10"],
  35:     "ai_sovereignty": ["bill_id", "jurisdiction", "year"],
  36:     "canada_us": ["jurisdiction", "treaty_id", "year"],
  37:     "climate": ["jurisdiction", "policy_id", "target_year"],
  38:     "defense": ["program_id", "jurisdiction", "year"],
  39:     "housing": ["jurisdiction", "policy_id", "year"],
  40:     "trade": ["hs_code", "jurisdiction", "year"],
  41:     "workforce": ["jurisdiction", "indicator_id", "year"],
  42: }
  43: 
  44: # Last-resort URL when a template has empty T1. Per Codex iter-5 P2 accepted-
  45: # remaining: this is acceptable for v1 (all 8 current templates have T1);
  46: # future templates should fail-loud, deferred to follow-up.
  47: _EMPTY_T1_FALLBACK = "https://www.canada.ca/en/research.html"
  48: 
  49: 
  50: def _anchor_for(template_id: str, frame_id: str, query_slug: str) -> str:
  51:     """Stable, unique anchor: <template>:<frame>:<slug_prefix>:<sha256_8>.
  52: 
  53:     Used as a secondary stable id (not the retrieval locator — url_pattern is).
  54:     Collision-safe for any realistic curator workload (2^32 combinations).
  55:     """
  56:     h = hashlib.sha256(
  57:         f"{template_id}|{frame_id}|{query_slug}".encode("utf-8")
  58:     ).hexdigest()[:8]
  59:     return f"{template_id}:{frame_id}:{query_slug[:40]}:{h}"
  60: 
  61: 
  62: def _concrete_url_for_entity(frame_idx: int, source_tiers: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  63:     """Concrete http(s) URL for this entity, rotated through T1 by frame index.
  64: 
  65:     M-56's `_fetch_url_pattern()` treats this value as a literal URL, NOT a
  66:     regex (per Codex iter-4 P1 verification at frame_fetcher.py:780,1046).
  67:     Returning a regex would fail to fetch.
  68: 
  69:     Rotation: entity[i] uses T1[i % len(T1)]. Different frames retrieve
  70:     different roots; strict_verify later filters per-frame relevance.
  71:     """
  72:     t1 = source_tiers.get("T1") or []
  73:     if t1:
  74:         return t1[frame_idx % len(t1)]
  75:     return _EMPTY_T1_FALLBACK
  76: 
  77: 
  78: def build_v30_contract(
  79:     v6_template: dict[str, Any],
  80:     query_slug: str,
  81:     question: str | None = None,
  82: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
  83:     """Synthesize a v30.1 per_query_report_contract.{query_slug} dict from a v6 template.
  84: 
  85:     Args:
  86:         v6_template: loaded v6 template JSON (config/v6_templates/<id>.json)
  87:         query_slug: pipeline-A URL-safe slug (e.g. "clinical_glp1_t2dm")
  88:         question: reserved for future question-aware seeding; iter-1 implementation
  89:                   uses frame_id as entity_id basis.
  90: 
  91:     Returns:
  92:         {query_slug: <contract>} where <contract> has schema_version="v30.1",
  93:         required_entities, rendering_slots (dict-keyed by slot_id), and
  94:         section_order. Round-trips clean via load_report_contract_for_slug.
  95:     """
  96:     del question  # reserved; suppress unused-arg warning
  97:     template_id = v6_template.get("template_id", "")
  98:     frame_manifest = v6_template.get("frame_manifest") or []
  99:     source_tiers = v6_template.get("source_tiers") or {}
 100: 
 101:     entity_type = _TYPE_FOR_TEMPLATE.get(template_id, "policy")
 102:     required_fields = _REQUIRED_FIELDS_FOR_TEMPLATE.get(
 103:         template_id, ["jurisdiction", "year"]
 104:     )
 105: 
 106:     required_entities: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
 107:     rendering_slots: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
 108:     sections_seen: list[str] = []  # ordered, deduped
 109: 
 110:     for idx, frame in enumerate(frame_manifest):
 111:         frame_id = frame.get("frame_id", f"frame_{idx}")
 112:         frame_name = frame.get("frame_name", frame_id.replace("_", " ").title())
 113:         slot_id = f"{frame_id}_slot"
 114:         section = _section_for_frame(template_id, frame_id, idx)
 115:         if section not in sections_seen:
 116:             sections_seen.append(section)
 117: 
 118:         rendering_slots[slot_id] = {
 119:             "section": section,
 120:             "subsection_title": frame_name,
 121:             "ordering": idx + 1,
 122:             "required": True,
 123:         }
 124:         required_entities.append({
 125:             "id": f"{frame_id}_entity",
 126:             "type": entity_type,
 127:             "required_fields": list(required_fields),
 128:             "min_fields_for_completion": 1,
 129:             "rendering_slot": slot_id,
 130:             "url_pattern": _concrete_url_for_entity(idx, source_tiers),
 131:             "anchor": _anchor_for(template_id, frame_id, query_slug),
 132:         })
 133: 
 134:     contract = {
 135:         "schema_version": "v30.1",
 136:         "required_entities": required_entities,
 137:         "rendering_slots": rendering_slots,
 138:         "section_order": sections_seen,
 139:     }
 140:     return {query_slug: contract}
 141: 
 142: 
 143: def _section_for_frame(template_id: str, frame_id: str, idx: int) -> str:
 144:     """Group frames into 2-4 sections per template. Mechanical grouping; per-
 145:     template overrides can be added later via report_contract_override blocks.
 146:     """
 147:     # Per Codex iter-5 P2: section grouping is left mechanical-but-stable;
 148:     # template-specific overrides are a follow-up.
 149:     if template_id == "clinical":
 150:         section_map = {
 151:             "efficacy": "Efficacy",
 152:             "safety": "Safety",
 153:             "labelling": "Regulatory",
 154:             "post_market": "Post-market",
 155:             "subgroup": "Subgroups",
 156:         }
 157:     else:
 158:         # Policy templates default: split into Background / Findings / Implications.
 159:         if idx < 2:
 160:             return "Background"
 161:         if idx < 4:
 162:             return "Findings"
 163:         return "Implications"
 164:     return section_map.get(frame_id, "Other")

         # SURMOUNT-1/3/4 are indirect_for_t2d (obesity-only). The
         # generator reads these tags to avoid merging obesity-only
         # weight-loss estimates into direct T2D efficacy claims.
         # No-op when the template defines no labels for this slug.
         from src.polaris_graph.retrieval.primary_trial_expander import (
             label_rows_with_population_scope,
         )
         _m48_labeled_count = sum(
             1 for r in retrieval.evidence_rows
             if r.get("population_scope")
         )
         label_rows_with_population_scope(
             retrieval.evidence_rows, _template, q["slug"],
         )
         _m48_labeled_count_after = sum(
             1 for r in retrieval.evidence_rows
             if r.get("population_scope")
         )
         if _m48_labeled_count_after > _m48_labeled_count:
             _log(
                 f"[m48]         population_scope labeled "
                 f"{_m48_labeled_count_after - _m48_labeled_count} row(s)"
             )
 
         if len(retrieval.classified_sources) == 0:
             # BUG-B-101 fix: previously returned without any manifest,
             # so downstream couldn't tell the run happened at all.
             summary["status"] = "fail_no_sources"
             summary["error"] = "zero sources retrieved"
             run_cost = current_run_cost()
             abort_manifest = _base_manifest_envelope(
                 run_id=run_id, q=q, retrieval=retrieval, run_cost=run_cost,
             )
             abort_manifest.update({
                 "status": "abort_no_sources",
                 "error": "zero sources retrieved",
             })
             abort_manifest = augment_v6_manifest(
                 abort_manifest,
                 external_run_id=q.get("external_run_id"),
                 decision_id=q.get("decision_id"),
                 query_slug=q.get("slug"),

 # I-arch-001a: week-1 template→scope_domain mapping. Per Codex iter-3 APPROVE
 # of brief. Per-domain expansion (real scope_templates for 4 new policy

 TEMPLATE_TO_SCOPE_DOMAIN = {
     "ai_sovereignty": "policy",
     "canada_us": "policy",

     "clinical": "clinical",
     "defense": "policy",
     "housing": "policy",

 }
 
 
 def _derive_slug(template_id: str, question: str) -> str:
     """Deterministic URL-safe slug for pipeline-A run_dir nesting.
 
     Pipeline-A reads q['slug']; this produces a stable, human-readable
     identifier per (template, question) pair. UUID provides uniqueness
     via the artifact_dir parent — slug itself doesn't need to be unique.
     """
     base = f"{template_id}_{question[:60]}"
     cleaned = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9_]+", "_", base.lower()).strip("_")
     return cleaned[:120] or "untitled"
 
 
 @dramatiq.actor(max_retries=ENQUEUE_MAX_RETRIES, time_limit=30 * 60 * 1000)
 def enqueue_research_run(run_id: str, request_payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
     """Execute a research run via pipeline-A. Idempotent on run_id.
 
     Stub-mode path: when run_store has no row for run_id (tests use
     .fn() directly without insert_run), returns deterministic noop
     without DB writes — preserves I-phase0-005 stub-mode semantics.
 
     Production path: marks in_progress, builds q-dict with v6 fields,
     invokes scripts.run_honest_sweep_r3.run_one_query, parses the
     manifest.json pipeline-A writes, and dispatches to
     mark_completed / mark_aborted / mark_failed per pipeline_status.
     """
     # Stub-mode preservation
     if run_store.get_run(run_id) is None:
         return {"run_id": run_id, "status": "completed", "echo": request_payload}
 
     run_store.mark_in_progress(run_id)
     decision_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
     output_root = Path(os.environ.get("POLARIS_V6_OUTPUT_ROOT", "outputs/v6_runs"))
     artifact_dir_root = output_root / run_id
     artifact_dir_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 
     template_id = request_payload.get("template", "")
     question = request_payload.get("question", "")
     domain = TEMPLATE_TO_SCOPE_DOMAIN.get(template_id, "policy")
     slug = _derive_slug(template_id, question)
 
     # v6 fields flow through q-dict (NO os.environ mutation per iter-2 P1.2)
     q: dict[str, Any] = {
         "domain": domain,
         "slug": slug,
         "question": question,
         "external_run_id": run_id,
         "decision_id": decision_id,
         "v6_mode": True,
         "out_root_override": str(artifact_dir_root),
         "template_id": template_id,
     }
 
+    # I-arch-001b: synthesize v30.1 contract patch from v6 template's
+    # frame_manifest. Pipeline-A merges this into the scope template's
+    # per_query_report_contract before compile_frame / load_report_contract_for_slug.
+    # Failure is graceful (logger.warning) — pipeline-A handles missing
+    # contract via legacy no-contract path.
+    try:
+        from polaris_v6.templates.registry import load_template
+        from src.polaris_graph.v30_contract_synthesizer import build_v30_contract
+
+        v6_tmpl = load_template(template_id).model_dump()
+        q["v30_contract_patch"] = build_v30_contract(v6_tmpl, slug, question)
+        logger.info(
+            "[actor] v30_contract_patch synthesized run_id=%s template_id=%s slug=%s entities=%d",
+            run_id,
+            template_id,
+            slug,
+            len(q["v30_contract_patch"][slug]["required_entities"]),
+        )
+    except FileNotFoundError as exc:
+        logger.warning(
+            "[actor] v6 template not found template_id=%s run_id=%s; "
+            "pipeline-A will run on legacy no-contract path: %s",
+            template_id,
+            run_id,
+            exc,
+        )
+    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — synthesizer failure must not block runtime
+        logger.warning(
+            "[actor] v30_contract_patch synthesis FAILED run_id=%s template_id=%s "
+            "slug=%s: %s; pipeline-A on legacy no-contract path",
+            run_id,
+            template_id,
+            slug,
+            exc,
+            exc_info=True,
+        )
+
     run_store.set_pipeline_meta(
         run_id,
         query_slug=slug,
         artifact_dir=str(artifact_dir_root),
         decision_id=decision_id,
     )
 
     try:
         from scripts.run_honest_sweep_r3 import run_one_query
 
         summary = asyncio.run(run_one_query(q, artifact_dir_root))
     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — actor must record any pipeline crash
         logger.exception("[actor] pipeline-A raised for run_id=%s", run_id)
         run_store.mark_failed(run_id, f"pipeline_exception: {type(exc).__name__}: {exc}")
         raise
 
     # Parse pipeline-A's manifest.json — written at every exit path
     manifest_path = artifact_dir_root / "manifest.json"
     if not manifest_path.is_file():
         run_store.mark_failed(
             run_id, "manifest_missing: pipeline-A returned without writing manifest.json"
         )
         return summary
     try:
         manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
     except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
         run_store.mark_failed(run_id, f"manifest_invalid: {exc}")
         return summary
 
     pipeline_status = manifest.get("status") or "error_unexpected"
     manifest_run_id = manifest.get("run_id")
     cost_usd = manifest.get("cost_usd")
     if cost_usd is None:
         cost_usd = summary.get("cost_usd")
     try:
         cost_usd_f = float(cost_usd) if cost_usd is not None else None
     except (TypeError, ValueError):
         cost_usd_f = None
 
     run_store.set_pipeline_meta(run_id, manifest_run_id=manifest_run_id)
 
     if pipeline_status == "success" or pipeline_status.startswith("partial_"):
         run_store.mark_completed(
             run_id, summary, pipeline_status=pipeline_status, cost_usd=cost_usd_f
         )
     elif pipeline_status.startswith("abort_"):
         run_store.mark_aborted(
             run_id,
             pipeline_status=pipeline_status,
             abort_reason=manifest.get("error") or pipeline_status,
             cost_usd=cost_usd_f,
         )
     elif pipeline_status.startswith("error_"):
         run_store.mark_failed(
             run_id, f"pipeline_error: {pipeline_status}: {manifest.get('error', '')}"
         )
     else:
         run_store.mark_failed(run_id, f"unknown_pipeline_status: {pipeline_status!r}")
     return summary

One integration detail stands out for verification: `actors.py` imports the synthesizer through `src.polaris_graph...`, while the test imports `polaris_graph...`. I’m checking whether that is an accepted local pattern or a packaging/runtime risk.

"""
polaris graph — clean-room research pipeline.

Uses Qwen 3.5 Plus via OpenRouter for all LLM calls.
Reuses battle-tested search/fetch infrastructure from src/tools/.
"""

__all__ = [
    "run_research",
]


async def run_research(
    vector_id: str,
    query: str,
    application: str,
    region: str,
    stage: int = 1,
    max_iterations: int = 3,
    max_execution_minutes: int = 30,
):
    """Entry point for polaris graph research pipeline.

    Routes to v3/v2/v1 based on PG_GRAPH_VERSION env var.
    """
    import os
    graph_version = os.getenv("PG_GRAPH_VERSION", "v1")
    if graph_version == "v3":
        from src.polaris_graph.graph_v3 import build_and_run_v3 as build_and_run
    else:
        from src.polaris_graph.graph import build_and_run

    return await build_and_run(
        vector_id=vector_id,
        query=query,
        application=application,
        region=region,
        stage=stage,
        max_iterations=max_iterations,
        max_execution_minutes=max_execution_minutes,
    )

  37:     if not path.exists():
  38:         raise FileNotFoundError(f"Template content not found: {path}")

  44:     if not TEMPLATES_DIR.exists():
  45:         return []
  46:     return sorted(p.stem for p in TEMPLATES_DIR.glob("*.json"))

   1: """M-55 (2026-04-23): V30 frame compiler (query → CompiledFrame).
   2: 
   3: V30 Report Contract Architecture Layer 2a. Codex V30 plan pass-1
   4: CONDITIONAL-no-blockers; M-55 was root_cause_approved_with_revision
   5: (Codex revision #1/#7: "compiler tests must prove arbitrary entity
   6: types and slot types compile without code changes").
   7: 
   8: ## Role in the architecture
   9: 
  10: M-54 provides the static YAML-shape validator. M-55 is the
  11: compilation stage: given `(research_question, template, slug)` it
  12: emits a `CompiledFrame` that carries:
  13: 
  14: - The resolved `ReportContract` (from M-54 loader).
  15: - Per-entity `EvidenceBinding` — how to retrieve and bind evidence
  16:   for each required entity (DOI / PMID / url_pattern / anchor
  17:   selected in priority order).
  18: - Compilation warnings (e.g. schema-version forward-compat notice).
  19: - The research_question text that drove compilation.
  20: - A deterministic rendering order (by section, ordering, entity id).
  21: 
  22: M-56 (deterministic DOI/PMID/Unpaywall retriever) consumes
  23: `CompiledFrame.evidence_bindings`. M-57 (outline instantiation)
  24: consumes `CompiledFrame.contract.rendering_slots`. M-58 (slot-bound
  25: generation) consumes both bindings and slots.
  26: 
  27: ## Codex review revisions woven in
  28: 
  29: - **#7 (M-62 generalization)**: compiler is entity-type-agnostic
  30:   AND slot-id/section/ordering-agnostic. `statute`,
  31:   `dft_primary`, `court_decision` entity types + arbitrary slot
  32:   ids, section names, and slot orderings all compile without
  33:   code changes. (The schema has no slot-TYPE vocabulary — that was
  34:   stale plan wording; the actual contract is shape-agnostic over
  35:   ids, section labels, and orderings.) Only two universal contracts
  36:   enforced:
  37:     1. Entity must have at least one identifier (doi/pmid/url_pattern/anchor).
  38:     2. Schema-version unknowns become warnings, not errors.
  39: - **#1/#7**: no per-type hardcoding of required_fields vocabulary.
  40:   The compiler propagates whatever the template declares.
  41: 
  42: ## Non-determinism guard (Codex plan review note)
  43: 
  44: Same input → same output. The compiler does not call networks,
  45: does not use wall-clock time, does not depend on dict iteration
  46: order. Ordering is sorted explicitly.
  47: 
  48: ## Descoped at M-55
  49: 
  50: **Domain-inheritance / contract composition** (V30 plan §M-55 test
  51: coverage "domain-inheritance works"): not implemented. Rationale:
  52: V30 ships exactly one slug (`clinical_tirzepatide_t2dm`). There is
  53: no second slug yet that would benefit from `extends:` composition,
  54: and implementing a template-inheritance resolver before the second
  55: concrete use-case would be speculative abstraction.
  56: 
  57: When a second slug lands (e.g. `clinical_tirzepatide_hfpef` sharing
  58: most entities with T2DM but overriding SURPASS-6), inheritance
  59: resolution can be added here with the concrete requirements known.
  60: Until then, per-slug contracts remain self-contained — the M-62
  61: non-clinical generalization guard will exercise a fresh slug, not
  62: an inherited one.
  63: 
  64: This descope supersedes the M-54 report_contract.py docstring's
  65: prospective "belongs in M-55" note.
  66: """
  67: from __future__ import annotations
  68: 
  69: from dataclasses import dataclass
  70: from typing import Any
  71: 
  72: from .report_contract import (
  73:     ContractSchemaError,
  74:     ReportContract,
  75:     RequiredEntity,
  76:     get_known_schema_versions,
  77:     load_report_contract_for_slug,
  78: )
  79: 
  80: 
  81: class FrameCompilerError(ValueError):
  82:     """Raised when a contract is structurally valid (passes M-54)
  83:     but cannot be compiled into a frame (e.g. entity has no
  84:     identifier). Separate from ContractSchemaError to let callers
  85:     distinguish YAML-shape failures from compilation-stage failures."""
  86: 
  87:     def __init__(self, *, entity_id: str | None, reason: str) -> None:
  88:         loc = f"entity_id={entity_id!r}" if entity_id else "compiler"
  89:         super().__init__(f"frame compiler error at {loc}: {reason}")
  90:         self.entity_id = entity_id
  91:         self.reason = reason
  92: 
  93: 
  94: @dataclass(frozen=True)
  95: class EvidenceBinding:
  96:     """Per-entity compiled binding: how retrieval (M-56) should
  97:     resolve the entity, and how the slot-fill stage (M-58) should
  98:     account for it.
  99: 
 100:     `primary_identifier` is the best locator per priority order
 101:     (doi > pmid > url_pattern > anchor). `secondary_identifiers`
 102:     carries the remainder, so M-56 can fall back deterministically
 103:     without re-consulting the contract.
 104:     """
 105: 
 106:     entity_id: str
 107:     entity_type: str
 108:     primary_identifier: str
 109:     secondary_identifiers: tuple[str, ...]
 110:     rendering_slot: str
 111:     required_fields: tuple[str, ...]
 112:     min_fields_for_completion: int
 113: 
 114: 
 115: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 116: class CompiledFrame:
 117:     """Output of M-55 frame compiler.
 118: 
 119:     Carries the resolved contract plus compilation-time data needed
 120:     by M-56 / M-57 / M-58. Pure value object: no mutation, no I/O.
 121:     """
 122: 
 123:     slug: str
 124:     schema_version: str
 125:     research_question: str
 126:     contract: ReportContract
 127:     evidence_bindings: tuple[EvidenceBinding, ...]
 128:     ordered_entity_ids: tuple[str, ...]
 129:     warnings: tuple[str, ...]
 130: 
 131:     def bindings_by_entity_id(self) -> dict[str, EvidenceBinding]:
 132:         return {b.entity_id: b for b in self.evidence_bindings}
 133: 
 134:     def bindings_by_slot(self) -> dict[str, list[EvidenceBinding]]:
 135:         out: dict[str, list[EvidenceBinding]] = {}
 136:         for b in self.evidence_bindings:
 137:             out.setdefault(b.rendering_slot, []).append(b)
 138:         return out
 139: 
 140: 
 141: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 142: # Identifier priority order.
 143: # Same priority used by M-56 retriever fallback chain so compiler
 144: # and retriever agree on which locator is "primary".
 145: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 146: _IDENTIFIER_PRIORITY: tuple[str, ...] = ("doi", "pmid", "url_pattern", "anchor")
 147: 
 148: 
 149: def compile_frame(
 150:     research_question: str,
 151:     template: dict[str, Any] | None,
 152:     slug: str,
 153: ) -> CompiledFrame | None:
 154:     """M-55 public accessor: compile a per-query frame for one
 155:     research-question slug.
 156: 
 157:     Args:
 158:         research_question: The raw user question text. Pass-through;
 159:             retained in CompiledFrame for downstream prompt grounding.
 160:         template: Loaded scope template dict (yaml.safe_load output).
 161:         slug: Research-question slug (e.g. 'clinical_tirzepatide_t2dm').
 162: 
 163:     Returns:
 164:         CompiledFrame when the template has a contract for this slug.
 165:         None when no contract exists (backwards-compat with V28/V29
 166:         slugs that have not yet been migrated to V30 contracts).
 167: 
 168:     Raises:
 169:         ContractSchemaError: propagated from M-54 loader on YAML
 170:             shape malformation.
 171:         FrameCompilerError: raised at compile stage when a structurally
 172:             valid contract entity has no identifier (no doi, pmid,
 173:             url_pattern, or anchor).
 174: 
 175:     Determinism: same `(research_question, template, slug)` inputs
 176:     always produce the same CompiledFrame (no I/O, no wall-clock,
 177:     explicit sort on all iteration).
 178:     """
 179:     if not isinstance(research_question, str):
 180:         raise FrameCompilerError(
 181:             entity_id=None,
 182:             reason=(
 183:                 f"research_question must be str, got "
 184:                 f"{type(research_question).__name__}"
 185:             ),
 186:         )
 187: 
 188:     contract = load_report_contract_for_slug(template, slug)
 189:     if contract is None:
 190:         return None
 191: 
 192:     warnings: list[str] = []
 193: 
 194:     # ── Schema-version forward-compat check ──────────────────────
 195:     # M-54 accepts unknown schema_version at loader level; M-55 is
 196:     # where the warning surfaces so downstream consumers can decide
 197:     # whether to proceed or abort.
 198:     if contract.schema_version not in get_known_schema_versions():
 199:         warnings.append(
 200:             f"schema_version {contract.schema_version!r} unknown to "
 201:             f"runtime; known versions: "
 202:             f"{sorted(get_known_schema_versions())}. "
 203:             f"Compiler will proceed — downstream consumers should "
 204:             f"treat field semantics as best-effort."
 205:         )
 206: 
 207:     # ── Cross-section ordering policy ────────────────────────────
 208:     # Codex M-55 audit Medium: alphabetic-by-label is fragile to
 209:     # section rename/localization. When the contract declares
 210:     # `section_order`, honor it; otherwise fall back to alphabetic
 211:     # and emit a warning so future templates are nudged toward
 212:     # explicit ordering.
 213:     if contract.section_order is None:
 214:         warnings.append(
 215:             "contract has no explicit section_order; falling back "
 216:             "to alphabetic-by-label cross-section ordering. This is "
 217:             "fragile to section rename/localization — declare "
 218:             "`section_order: [...]` in the contract YAML for stable "
 219:             "cross-section rendering."
 220:         )
 221: 
 222:     # ── Deterministic entity ordering ────────────────────────────
 223:     ordered = _ordered_entities(contract)
 224: 
 225:     # ── Compile bindings (entity-type-agnostic per Codex rev #7) ─
 226:     bindings: list[EvidenceBinding] = []
 227:     for e in ordered:
 228:         bindings.append(_compile_binding(e))
 229: 
 230:     return CompiledFrame(
 231:         slug=contract.slug,
 232:         schema_version=contract.schema_version,
 233:         research_question=research_question,
 234:         contract=contract,
 235:         evidence_bindings=tuple(bindings),
 236:         ordered_entity_ids=tuple(e.id for e in ordered),
 237:         warnings=tuple(warnings),
 238:     )

   9: the mandatory content model that replaces V29's corpus-driven
  10: emergent-frame approach. See
  11: `outputs/audits/v29/true_root_cause_cross_review.md` for the

  13: 
  14: ## Layer 1 of 5
  15: 
  16: M-54 is the foundation: YAML schema + Python dataclasses + strict
  17: loader with precise error messages. Layer 2 (M-55 frame compiler)
  18: consumes this. Layer 3-5 consume the compiled contract.
  19: 
  20: ## Contract semantics (from Codex's framing)
  21: 
  22: A Report Contract has THREE parts per research-question slug:
  23: 1. schema_version — contract schema revision tracking
  24: 2. required_entities — list of entities that MUST be rendered:

  29: 
  30: Entity types at M-54 level (extensible at M-55 compiler):
  31: - pivotal_trial    — named clinical trial primary publication
  32: - mechanism_primary — pharmacology primary (clamp/PK/receptor)
  33: - regulatory       — jurisdiction-specific label/guidance/monograph
  34: 
  35: ## Strict loader contract
  36: 
  37: - Malformed YAML raises ContractSchemaError with precise field path.
  38: - Unknown entity types are NOT rejected at M-54 level (extensibility
  39:   requirement per Codex review #7: compiler must not hard-code entity
  40:   types). M-55 compiler + M-57/58 renderers are responsible for
  41:   per-type handling.
  42: - Missing required fields raise with path.
  43: - Schema-version mismatch is a WARNING (forward compatibility).

  52:   (only one slug exists in V30; adding `extends:` before a concrete

  65: # Codex M-63 REJECT Medium 3 fix: live retrieval assigns ids of

  74: class ContractSchemaError(ValueError):
  75:     """Raised when a report contract YAML cannot be loaded into valid
  76:     runtime types. Message includes the exact path inside the YAML
  77:     that failed."""
  78: 
  79:     def __init__(self, path: str, reason: str) -> None:
  80:         super().__init__(f"contract schema error at {path}: {reason}")
  81:         self.path = path
  82:         self.reason = reason
  83:

  85: @dataclass(frozen=True)
  86: class RequiredEntity:
  87:     """One required entity in the report contract.
  88: 
  89:     At M-54 level the schema is intentionally permissive on entity
  90:     type — per Codex revision #7 (M-62 generalization proof), the
  91:     compiler + renderers must handle arbitrary entity types without
  92:     code changes. This dataclass carries the raw YAML fields; type-
  93:     specific interpretation is left to M-55 compiler + downstream
  94:     consumers.
  95:     """
  96: 
  97:     id: str
  98:     type: str
  99:     required_fields: tuple[str, ...]
 100:     min_fields_for_completion: int
 101:     rendering_slot: str
 102:     # Optional identifier fields — interpretation depends on entity type
 103:     doi: str | None = None
 104:     pmid: int | str | None = None
 105:     url_pattern: str | None = None
 106:     # Optional metadata fields — passed through for renderer use
 107:     anchor: str | None = None
 108:     journal: str | None = None
 109:     year: int | None = None
 110:     population_scope: str | None = None
 111:     jurisdiction: str | None = None
 112:     label_name: str | None = None
 113:

 115: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 116: class RenderingSlot:
 117:     """Declarative slot spec: where the slot appears in the report and
 118:     in what order."""
 119: 
 120:     id: str
 121:     section: str
 122:     subsection_title: str
 123:     ordering: int
 124:     required: bool = True
 125: 
 126: 
 127: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 128: class ReportContract:
 129:     """Resolved report contract for one research-question slug.
 130: 
 131:     Produced by M-55 frame compiler; consumed by M-57 planner
 132:     + M-58 slot-bound generator + M-59 validator + M-60 gap renderer.
 133:     """
 134: 
 135:     slug: str
 136:     schema_version: str
 137:     required_entities: tuple[RequiredEntity, ...]
 138:     rendering_slots: tuple[RenderingSlot, ...]
 139:     # Optional explicit section ordering. When None the M-55 compiler
 140:     # falls back to alphabetic-by-label ordering and emits a warning.
 141:     # Fixes Codex M-55 audit Medium (cross-section order was fragile
 142:     # to section-label rename/localization).
 143:     section_order: tuple[str, ...] | None = None
 144: 
 145:     def entities_by_id(self) -> dict[str, RequiredEntity]:
 146:         return {e.id: e for e in self.required_entities}
 147: 
 148:     def slots_by_id(self) -> dict[str, RenderingSlot]:
 149:         return {s.id: s for s in self.rendering_slots}
 150: 
 151:     def entities_by_slot(self) -> dict[str, list[RequiredEntity]]:
 152:         """Slot id -> entities whose rendering_slot points to it.
 153:         Typically 1:1 but the schema allows multi-entity-per-slot
 154:         (e.g. a table row populated from multiple evidence rows)."""
 155:         out: dict[str, list[RequiredEntity]] = {}
 156:         for e in self.required_entities:
 157:             out.setdefault(e.rendering_slot, []).append(e)
 158:         return out
 159:

 163: # Forward-compat: if a template declares a newer schema_version than
 164: # the runtime knows, we WARN (via `schema_version_warnings`), not raise.
 165: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 166: _KNOWN_SCHEMA_VERSIONS = frozenset({"v30.1"})

 169: # Required top-level keys in the `required_entities[*]` object.

 176: _REQUIRED_SLOT_KEYS = {
 177:     "section", "subsection_title", "ordering",

 241: def _ordered_entities(contract: ReportContract) -> list[RequiredEntity]:
 242:     """Deterministic rendering order.
 243: 
 244:     Cross-section order:
 245:       - if `contract.section_order` is declared: sections sort by
 246:         their index in that tuple.
 247:       - else: alphabetic by section label (a warning is surfaced
 248:         by the compiler — see Codex M-55 audit Medium).
 249:     Within-section tiebreak: slot.ordering, then entity.id.
 250:     """
 251:     slot_by_id = contract.slots_by_id()
 252: 
 253:     if contract.section_order is not None:
 254:         section_rank = {s: i for i, s in enumerate(contract.section_order)}
 255:         # A section referenced by a slot but absent from section_order
 256:         # would already have raised at M-54 load. Defensive default:
 257:         # sort unknown sections after all declared sections.
 258:         max_rank = len(section_rank)
 259: 
 260:         def sort_key(e: RequiredEntity) -> tuple[int, int, str]:
 261:             slot = slot_by_id[e.rendering_slot]
 262:             return (
 263:                 section_rank.get(slot.section, max_rank),
 264:                 slot.ordering,
 265:                 e.id,
 266:             )
 267:     else:
 268:         # Alphabetic-by-label fallback. Warning emitted in compile_frame.
 269:         def sort_key(e: RequiredEntity) -> tuple[str | int, int, str]:  # type: ignore[misc]
 270:             slot = slot_by_id[e.rendering_slot]
 271:             return (slot.section, slot.ordering, e.id)
 272: 
 273:     return sorted(contract.required_entities, key=sort_key)

 276: def _compile_binding(entity: RequiredEntity) -> EvidenceBinding:
 277:     """Entity-type-AGNOSTIC binding compilation (Codex rev #7).
 278: 
 279:     Identifier priority (stable across all entity types):
 280:       1. DOI  — most universal stable identifier
 281:       2. PMID — stable for medical literature
 282:       3. url_pattern — for regulatory / web-hosted sources
 283:       4. anchor — for unpublished or not-yet-assigned-DOI trials
 284: 
 285:     At least one identifier must resolve. No identifier → raise
 286:     FrameCompilerError (M-54 permits missing all identifiers at
 287:     shape level because some edge cases may declare identifier
 288:     inline in required_fields; M-55 is where "must be retrievable"
 289:     becomes enforced).
 290:     """
 291:     candidates: list[str] = []
 292:     if entity.doi:
 293:         candidates.append(f"doi:{entity.doi}")
 294:     if entity.pmid is not None and entity.pmid != "" and entity.pmid != 0:
 295:         # Accept int or str PMID; reject 0/empty as non-identifier.
 296:         candidates.append(f"pmid:{entity.pmid}")
 297:     if entity.url_pattern:
 298:         candidates.append(f"url:{entity.url_pattern}")
 299:     if entity.anchor:
 300:         candidates.append(f"anchor:{entity.anchor}")
 301: 
 302:     if not candidates:
 303:         raise FrameCompilerError(
 304:             entity_id=entity.id,
 305:             reason=(
 306:                 "entity has no identifier (no doi, pmid, "
 307:                 "url_pattern, or anchor). M-56 retriever cannot "
 308:                 "resolve this entity. Add at least one identifier "
 309:                 "to the contract YAML."
 310:             ),
 311:         )
 312: 
 313:     return EvidenceBinding(
 314:         entity_id=entity.id,
 315:         entity_type=entity.type,
 316:         primary_identifier=candidates[0],
 317:         secondary_identifiers=tuple(candidates[1:]),
 318:         rendering_slot=entity.rendering_slot,
 319:         required_fields=entity.required_fields,
 320:         min_fields_for_completion=entity.min_fields_for_completion,
 321:     )
 322: 
 323: 
 324: def get_identifier_priority_order() -> tuple[str, ...]:
 325:     """Expose identifier priority for M-56 retriever to consult.
 326:     Returns (doi, pmid, url_pattern, anchor) — the order compiler
 327:     uses for primary_identifier selection."""
 328:     return _IDENTIFIER_PRIORITY

 730: def fetch_frame_entity(
 731:     binding: EvidenceBinding,
 732:     *,
 733:     client: httpx.Client | None = None,
 734: ) -> FrameRow:
 735:     """Deterministic frame-entity retriever.
 736: 
 737:     Given a compiled EvidenceBinding (from M-55), emit one FrameRow
 738:     with provenance_class, direct_quote, metadata, and retrieval
 739:     attempt log.
 740: 
 741:     Args:
 742:         binding: M-55 compiled binding with primary_identifier +
 743:             secondary_identifiers.
 744:         client: optional httpx.Client for DI (testing). When None,
 745:             a fresh client is created per call with _DEFAULT_TIMEOUT.
 746: 
 747:     Returns:
 748:         FrameRow — always non-None. A FRAME_GAP_UNRECOVERABLE row is
 749:         still a valid return — callers inspect `is_gap()` or
 750:         `provenance_class` to branch.
 751: 
 752:     Deterministic per design — same (binding, upstream API state) →
 753:     byte-identical FrameRow. No randomness, no wall-clock in payload.
 754:     """
 755:     owns_client = client is None
 756:     if client is None:
 757:         client = httpx.Client(timeout=_DEFAULT_TIMEOUT)
 758:     try:
 759:         return _fetch_frame_entity_inner(binding, client)
 760:     finally:
 761:         if owns_client:
 762:             client.close()
 763: 
 764: 
 765: def _fetch_frame_entity_inner(
 766:     binding: EvidenceBinding,
 767:     client: httpx.Client,
 768: ) -> FrameRow:
 769:     """Core dispatch: pick strategy by primary_identifier prefix."""
 770:     identifiers = _collect_identifiers(binding)

 772:     # URL-pattern-primary entities (regulatory): V30 Phase-2 M-66b-R
 773:     # lifts these from METADATA_ONLY to OPEN_ACCESS when content can

 775:     # CONDITIONAL-no-blockers approved this scope.

 777:         identifiers.get("doi") or identifiers.get("pmid")

 784:                 source="access_bypass",
 785:                 url=f"url_pattern:{fetched_url or url}",
 786:                 attempt_index=1,
 787:                 http_status=200,
 788:                 outcome="success",
 789:             ))
 790:             return FrameRow(
 791:                 entity_id=binding.entity_id,
 792:                 entity_type=binding.entity_type,
 793:                 rendering_slot=binding.rendering_slot,
 794:                 provenance_class=ProvenanceClass.OPEN_ACCESS,
 795:                 direct_quote=fetched_content,
 796:                 quote_source="url_pattern_fetch",
 797:                 doi=None,

 799:                 oa_pdf_url=None,
 800:                 url=fetched_url or url,
 801:                 title=None,
 802:                 authors=(),

 805:                 failure_reason=None,

1045: 
1046: def _collect_identifiers(binding: EvidenceBinding) -> dict[str, str]:
1047:     """Flatten primary + secondary identifiers into a {kind: value}
1048:     dict. Kinds: 'doi', 'pmid', 'url', 'anchor'."""
1049:     out: dict[str, str] = {}
1050:     for ident in (binding.primary_identifier, *binding.secondary_identifiers):
1051:         if ":" not in ident:
1052:             continue
1053:         kind, value = ident.split(":", 1)
1054:         out.setdefault(kind, value)
1055:     return out
1056: 
1057: 
1058: def _summarize_failure(attempts: list[RetrievalAttempt]) -> str:
1059:     """Compose a short failure_reason string from the attempt log.
1060:     Consumed by M-60 manifest rendering. Summarizes the FINAL
1061:     outcome per source (aggregates retry noise, while the full
1062:     chain remains visible via FrameRow.retrieval_attempts)."""
1063:     if not attempts:
1064:         return "no retrieval attempted (no resolvable identifier)"
1065:     # Collapse per-source by taking the last attempt for each
1066:     # source (which carries the terminal outcome).
1067:     final_by_source: dict[str, RetrievalAttempt] = {}
1068:     for a in attempts:
1069:         final_by_source[a.source] = a

 671: def _fetch_url_pattern(url: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
 672:     """Fetch content at `url` via AccessBypass. Returns
 673:     `(content, final_url)` or `("", "")` on failure.
 674: 
 675:     Deterministic-test seam: this function is the mockable
 676:     boundary for M-66b-R / M-66b-T tests (stub via
 677:     `monkeypatch.setattr("...frame_fetcher._fetch_url_pattern",
 678:     lambda u: ("stubbed content", u))`).
 679: 
 680:     AccessBypass.fetch_with_bypass is async; M-56 is sync. The
 681:     helper wraps the async call in asyncio.run(). If an event
 682:     loop is already running in the caller's thread (live server
 683:     context), we fall back to a fresh thread + new loop so this
 684:     helper is safe to invoke from any caller context.
 685:     """
 686:     if not url:
 687:         return "", ""
 688:     try:
 689:         import asyncio as _asyncio
 690:         from src.tools.access_bypass import AccessBypass
 691: 
 692:         async def _run() -> tuple[str, str]:
 693:             ab = AccessBypass()
 694:             result = await ab.fetch_with_bypass(url)
 695:             if result is None or not getattr(result, "success", False):
 696:                 return "", ""
 697:             content = getattr(result, "content", "") or ""
 698:             final_url = getattr(result, "url", "") or url
 699:             if not content:
 700:                 return "", ""
 701:             return content[:_M66_CONTENT_CAP], final_url
 702: 
 703:         try:
 704:             # Probe for a running loop. asyncio.get_running_loop
 705:             # raises RuntimeError when no loop is running (normal
 706:             # sync context); the no-warning way to ask.
 707:             _asyncio.get_running_loop()
 708:             # A loop IS running — spin a fresh one in a worker
 709:             # thread so we don't collide with it (e.g. live-server
 710:             # FastAPI context).
 711:             import concurrent.futures as _cf
 712: 
 713:             def _thread_run() -> tuple[str, str]:
 714:                 return _asyncio.run(_run())
 715: 
 716:             with _cf.ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=1) as ex:
 717:                 return ex.submit(_thread_run).result()
 718:         except RuntimeError:
 719:             # No running loop — asyncio.run will create one.
 720:             return _asyncio.run(_run())
 721:     except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001
 722:         # AccessBypass raised — don't propagate; M-56 treats as
 723:         # failed fetch and continues with whatever it has.
 724:         return "", ""
 725:

 728: # Layer 4 — Orchestrator

  e2e_playwright:
    name: e2e + a11y + perf (Playwright on Chromium)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint_format_typecheck_build
    steps:
      - name: checkout
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: setup_node
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: "22"
          cache: "npm"
          cache-dependency-path: web/package-lock.json

      - name: setup_python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.13"
          cache: "pip"

      - name: install_python_dependencies
        working-directory: ${{ github.workspace }}
        run: |
          python -m pip install --upgrade pip
          pip install -r requirements.txt

      - name: install_npm_dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: install_playwright_chromium
        run: npx playwright install --with-deps chromium

      - name: start_fastapi_backend
        working-directory: ${{ github.workspace }}
        run: |
          PYTHONPATH=src nohup python -m uvicorn polaris_v6.api.app:app \
            --host 127.0.0.1 --port 8000 \
            > /tmp/fastapi.log 2>&1 &
          # Wait for /health to respond.
          for i in {1..30}; do
            if curl -fs http://127.0.0.1:8000/health > /dev/null; then
              echo "backend ready"
              exit 0
            fi
            sleep 1
          done
          echo "backend failed to start"
          cat /tmp/fastapi.log
          exit 1

      - name: build_and_start_next
        run: |
          npm run build
          nohup npx next start -p 3738 > /tmp/next.log 2>&1 &
          # Wait for /dashboard to respond.
          for i in {1..30}; do
            if curl -fs http://127.0.0.1:3738/dashboard > /dev/null; then
              echo "frontend ready"
              exit 0
            fi
            sleep 1
          done
          echo "frontend failed to start"
          cat /tmp/next.log
          exit 1

      - name: run_e2e_inspector
        env:
          SCREENSHOT_BASE_URL: http://127.0.0.1:3738
          POLARIS_V6_BACKEND_URL: http://127.0.0.1:8000

          POLARIS_V6_BACKEND_URL: http://127.0.0.1:8000
        run: npx playwright test --project=chromium tests/e2e/performance.spec.ts

  verify_pip_resolution:
    # F-22 (cycle-7 P1.1 prevention): catches pip dependency conflicts
    # before they reach pytest_v6_backend or the production Dockerfile.
    # Cycle-7 caught F-17's protobuf>=6.33.5 pin breaking against
    # google-generativeai's transitive protobuf<5.0.0 constraint.
    name: pip install --dry-run (catch ResolutionImpossible early)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint_format_typecheck_build
    steps:
      - name: checkout
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: setup_python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.13"

      - name: pip_dry_run_legacy_requirements
        # If this fails, requirements.txt has a conflict; production
        # Dockerfile build would fail in the same way.
        run: pip install --dry-run -r requirements.txt

      - name: pip_dry_run_v6_requirements
        # Verify the v6 backend's pinned set also resolves cleanly.
        run: pip install --dry-run -r requirements-v6.txt

  pytest_v6_backend:
    name: pytest tests/v6/ (Phase 0 backend coverage)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: [lint_format_typecheck_build, verify_pip_resolution]
    defaults:
      run:
        working-directory: ${{ github.workspace }}
    steps:
      - name: checkout
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: setup_python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.13"
          cache: "pip"

      # Cycle-3 audit P2.3 (outputs/audits/continuous/bb60495_audit.md):
      # tests/v6/test_*_middleware.py + test_actors.py + test_broker.py +
      # test_otel_init.py use pytest.importorskip against dramatiq +
      # opentelemetry deps. Without -v6.txt installed they SILENTLY SKIP
      # (LAW II violation). This job uses requirements-v6.txt as the
      # canonical pin source for v6 backend code.
      - name: install_v6_dependencies
        run: |
          python -m pip install --upgrade pip
          pip install -r requirements-v6.txt

      - name: run_pytest_v6
        env:
          PYTHONPATH: src
        # `-q` keeps output tight; `--strict-markers` fails on undefined
        # markers; `--no-header` removes pytest banner from CI logs.
        # Acceptance suite (tests/v6/acceptance/) is excluded — it requires
        # a live broker; covered by tests/v6/acceptance/test_dramatiq_acceptance.py
        # which runs in its own integration job once Vast.ai cluster is live.
        run: |
          pytest tests/v6/ \
            --ignore=tests/v6/acceptance \
            -q --strict-markers --no-header

#!/bin/bash
set -e

echo "=== POLARIS Sovereign Deep Research Platform ==="
echo "Version: ${POLARIS_VERSION:-0.9.0}"
echo "Mode: ${POLARIS_DEPLOYMENT_MODE:-cloud}"
echo "================================================"

# Verify required environment variables
REQUIRED_VARS=""
if [ "${POLARIS_DEPLOYMENT_MODE}" != "sovereign" ]; then
    REQUIRED_VARS="OPENROUTER_API_KEY"
fi

for var in $REQUIRED_VARS; do
    if [ -z "${!var}" ]; then
        echo "ERROR: Required environment variable $var is not set"
        exit 1
    fi
done

# Create necessary directories
mkdir -p /app/outputs/polaris_graph /app/logs /app/state /app/data

case "${1:-serve}" in
    serve)
        echo "Starting POLARIS web server on port 8000..."
        exec python -m uvicorn scripts.live_server:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000 --workers 1
        ;;
    sweep)
        # Pipeline A — the hardened honest-rebuild sweep orchestrator.
        # See BUG-B-1..B-5 in logs/bug_log.md for the 5-round audit history.
        echo "Running POLARIS pipeline A (honest-rebuild sweep)..."
        shift
        exec python -m scripts.run_honest_sweep_r3 "$@"
        ;;
    research)
        # BUG-M-208 (open, 2026-04-18): pipeline C is frozen and this
        # entry point is broken. scripts/full_cycle.py imports
        # scripts/run_ragas_v3.py and scripts/final_audit.py which
        # no longer exist. Disposition (retire/repair/leave) tracked
        # in src/orchestration/FROZEN_SINCE_2026-03-16.md.
        # Until that decision is made, refuse this command loudly
        # rather than hand users a broken crash.
        cat >&2 <<'DEPRECATION'
ERROR: The 'research' subcommand routes through pipeline C
(scripts/full_cycle.py) which is FROZEN and PARTIALLY BROKEN as of
2026-04-18. It imports scripts/run_ragas_v3.py and scripts/final_audit.py
which do not exist in this repo.

Use instead:
    docker run polaris sweep --only <query_slug>     # pipeline A (hardened)
    docker run polaris serve                          # pipeline B (UI)

Or if you truly need the legacy research CLI, see
    src/orchestration/FROZEN_SINCE_2026-03-16.md
for the retire/repair/leave decision tree.
DEPRECATION
        exit 2
        ;;
    preflight)
        echo "Running preflight checks..."
        exec python -m scripts.pg_preflight
        ;;
    shell)
        echo "Starting interactive shell..."
        exec /bin/bash
        ;;
    *)
        echo "Unknown command: $1"
        echo "Usage: docker run polaris [serve|sweep|preflight|shell]"
        echo "  serve     — pipeline B (FastAPI UI, default)"
        echo "  sweep     — pipeline A (honest-rebuild sweep; pass --only <slug> for a single query)"
        echo "  preflight — environment check"
        echo "  shell     — interactive bash"

        echo "NOTE: the legacy 'research' subcommand is frozen and broken;"

async def fake_run_one_query(q, out_root):
    captured.update(q)
    out_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    (out_root / 'manifest.json').write_text(json.dumps(manifest) + '\\n', encoding='utf-8')
    return {'manifest': manifest, 'status': 'success', 'cost_usd': 0.0}
